##  About the job

** Company Description:  **

Wayzim is an industry-leading supplier of intelligent logistics equipment,
intelligent vision systems and industrial sensors. One of the few
international companies that have the integrated capabilities to research,
develop, design, and manufacture intelligent logistics equipment systems and
key components.

We have a strong interest in finding the best employees for our company and in
their being committed to us for the long term. Naturally, it is our employees
who inspire our customers and partners. At Wayzim Hungary , you can take your
career to new heights in a challenging and exciting global environment.

** Job Description  **

** As a Sales Engineer your main functions/tasks will be:  **

· You are together with the Sales Manager and other team members to make an
important contribution to the sales success in the pre-contract phase of a
project. Develop technical proposals (quotations, presentations, etc.) and
economic proposals (budgets, prices…) to assigned opportunities.

· You are a member of the solution team, and your main tasks are to identify
customer needs and to translate these into a winning technical solution /
concept, which consists of the right balance between advanced technology and a
competitive price.

· You are the central key person on technical and concept specification in
relation to the project by cooperating with the team in HQ.

· You will work with partners, when necessary, in order to provide a complete
solution.

· You will play an important role in the hand-over of the project to the
execution team.

** **

** Job Requirements:  **

· You have a Bachelor or Master in relevant study (Industrial Engineering,
Mechanical Engineering, Automation, Electro-mechanical Engineering, Logistical
engineering or similar discipline).

· Preferably you have 3+ years relevant working experiences.

· You are a good listener and communicator, creative and driven to win.

· You have a high degree of initiative and you are a team play who is enjoying
working in an international team

· You are willing to travel internationally.

Posted on Feb 28, 2024.

See more
